You can enjoy the leisure in the courtyard and go out to feel the bustle of the city. Laomendong is particularly lively at night, and the lantern festival is also very beautiful. On weekends at 19:00, hotel guests can also watch Kunqu opera performances in the Mustard Seed Garden.

The hotel is close to the northeast gate of Laomen, and it is convenient to take a taxi. In addition, it is also very close to major attractions, such as Little West Lake, Confucius Temple, Zhanyuan (Taiping Heavenly Kingdom), and China Gate: they can all be reached by citywalk.

There are a lot of leisure and food in the scenic area. You can get a massage when you are tired. If you are hungry, you can try the must-eat list or Internet celebrity snacks.
